# A bit of (directory enumeration) theory 
# -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
#
# Web server directory enumeration represents the process by which a low 
# skilled attacker can identify existing directories present on the server.
# 
# JBroFuzz achieves this by checking for the existence of the following 
# directories.
#
# Any line in this file is regarded as a comment if it begins with a '#' (yes, 
# you can brake JBroFuzz if you fuzz this file!)
# 
# Special characters will be encoded by JBroFuzz. As an example, a line entry
# of 'li ve' will become 'li%20ve'
#
# Special thanks go to james (at) uncon sittinglittleduck com 
# Continue to look for directories out there!
#
# Copyright (C) 2007 subere (at) uncon org
# Version 0.5
